2019-10-12 23:24:06 东都大白兔
Mat translate(const Mat& src, int dx, int dy){	Mat ans_img = Mat::zeros(src.cols, src.rows, src.type());	for (int x = 0; x < src.cols; x++)	{		for (int y = 0; y < src.rows; y++)		{			if (x - dx < 0 || y - dy < 0 || x - dx >= src.cols || y - dy >= src.rows)			{				for (int c = 0; c < 3; c++)				{					ans_img.at<Vec3b>(x, y)[c] = saturate_cast<uchar>(0);				}			}			else			{				for (int c = 0; c < 3; c++)				{					ans_img.at<Vec3b>(x, y)[c] = src.at<Vec3b>(x - dx, y - dy)[c];				}			}		}		return ans_img;	}}

Mat translate(const Mat& src, int dx, int dy){	Mat ans_img = Mat::zeros(src.cols, src.rows, src.type());	for (int x = 0; x < src.cols; x++)	{		for (int y = 0; y < src.rows; y++)		{			if (x - dx < 0 || y - dy < 0 || x - dx >= src.cols || y - dy >= src.rows)			{				for (int c = 0; c < 3; c++)				{					ans_img.at<Vec3b>(x, y)[c] = saturate_cast<uchar>(0);				}			}			else			{				for (int c = 0; c < 3; c++)				{					ans_img.at<Vec3b>(x, y)[c] = saturate_cast<uchar>(src.at<Vec3b>(x-dx, y-dy)[c]);				}			}		}			}	return ans_img;}

# 输出图片import scipy import cv2from fractions import Fractiondef showimage(data):    this_image = data    this_image = this_image.reshape(28, 28)    plt.imshow(this_image, cmap=plt.cm.binary)    plt.show()def pred_image(file):    image = scipy.misc.imread(file)    im_resized = scipy.misc.imresize(image, (28, 28))    # print(im_resized)    im_gray = cv2.cvtColor(im_resized, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)    im_gray = np.array(im_gray).reshape((1, 28*28))[0] / 255.0    im_reverse = 1 - im_gray    showimage(im_reverse)    return(im_reverse)path = "11.jpg"try_image = pred_image(path)

2019-12-19 19:35:15 17—衡水 吕程
Mat getmyHomographMat(Mat& lastPart, Mat& curPart) {	Mat image1, image2;	cvtColor(lastPart, image1, CV_RGB2GRAY);	cvtColor(curPart, image2, CV_RGB2GRAY);	Ptr<xfeatures2d::SURF> detector = xfeatures2d::SURF::create(2000);	vector<KeyPoint> keyPoint1, keyPoint2;	Mat imageDesc1, imageDesc2;	detector->detectAndCompute(image1, Mat(), keyPoint1, imageDesc1);	detector->detectAndCompute(image2, Mat(), keyPoint2, imageDesc2);	FlannBasedMatcher matcher;	vector<vector<DMatch> > matchePoints;	vector<DMatch> GoodMatchePoints;	set< pair<int, int>>  matches;	vector<Mat> train_desc(1, imageDesc1);	matcher.add(train_desc);	matcher.train();	matcher.knnMatch(imageDesc2, matchePoints, 2);	for (int i = 0; i < matchePoints.size(); i++)	{		if (matchePoints[i][0].distance < 0.5 * matchePoints[i][1].distance)		{			GoodMatchePoints.push_back(matchePoints[i][0]);			matches.insert(make_pair(matchePoints[i][0].queryIdx, matchePoints[i][0].trainIdx));		}	}	//cout << "1->2 good 匹配点数目：" << GoodMatchePoints.size() << endl;	//可选是否进行二次特征点匹配筛选#if 1	FlannBasedMatcher matcher2;	matchePoints.clear();	vector<Mat> train_desc2(1, imageDesc2);	matcher2.add(train_desc2);	matcher2.train();	matcher2.knnMatch(imageDesc1, matchePoints, 2);	for (int i = 0; i < matchePoints.size(); i++)	{		if (matchePoints[i][0].distance < 0.5 * matchePoints[i][1].distance)		{			if (matches.find(make_pair(matchePoints[i][0].trainIdx, matchePoints[i][0].queryIdx)) == matches.end())			{				GoodMatchePoints.push_back(DMatch(matchePoints[i][0].trainIdx, matchePoints[i][0].queryIdx, matchePoints[i][0].distance));			}		}	}	cout << "1->2 & 2->1 good 匹配点数目：" << GoodMatchePoints.size() << endl;#endif	vector<Point2f> imagePoints1, imagePoints2;	for (int i = 0; i < GoodMatchePoints.size(); i++)	{		imagePoints2.push_back(keyPoint2[GoodMatchePoints[i].queryIdx].pt);		imagePoints1.push_back(keyPoint1[GoodMatchePoints[i].trainIdx].pt);	}	return findHomography(imagePoints1, imagePoints2, CV_RANSAC);}

2019-12-19 20:02:46 17—衡水 吕程
Mat getmyHomographMat(Mat& lastPart, Mat& curPart) {	Mat image1, image2;	cvtColor(lastPart, image1, CV_RGB2GRAY);	cvtColor(curPart, image2, CV_RGB2GRAY);	Ptr<ORB> orb = ORB::create(10000);	orb->setFastThreshold(0);	vector<KeyPoint> keyPoint1, keyPoint2;	Mat imageDesc11, imageDesc22;	orb->detectAndCompute(image1, Mat(), keyPoint1, imageDesc11);	orb->detectAndCompute(image2, Mat(), keyPoint2, imageDesc22);	Mat imageDesc1(imageDesc11.size(), CV_32F);	imageDesc11.convertTo(imageDesc1, CV_32F);	Mat imageDesc2(imageDesc22.size(), CV_32F);	imageDesc22.convertTo(imageDesc2, CV_32F);	BFMatcher matcher(NORM_HAMMING);	vector<DMatch> matches_all, matches_gms;	matcher.match(imageDesc1, imageDesc2, matches_all);	std::vector<bool> vbInliers;	gms_matcher gms(keyPoint1, image1.size(), keyPoint2, image2.size(), matches_all);	int num_inliers = gms.GetInlierMask(vbInliers, false, false);	cout << "Get total " << num_inliers << " matches." << endl;	for (size_t i = 0; i < vbInliers.size(); ++i)	{		if (vbInliers[i] == true)		{			matches_gms.push_back(matches_all[i]);		}	}	vector<Point2f> imagePoints1, imagePoints2;	for (int i = 0; i < matches_gms.size(); i++)	{		imagePoints2.push_back(keyPoint2[matches_gms[i].queryIdx].pt);		imagePoints1.push_back(keyPoint1[matches_gms[i].trainIdx].pt);	}	return findHomography(imagePoints1, imagePoints2, CV_RANSAC);}
